In short, people like me who never give bad reviews and are too lazy to write reviews are really uncomfortable. The overall feeling is that they are not up to the five-star service at all. It is said that the turnover rate of hotel staff is high, and quite a lot of them rely on interns. The hotel service is so professional and requires experience. Anyway, every detail reveals confusion and confusion. Will not come again in the future.
